################################################################################
# 文件 1/3: debug助手py2exe.py
################################################################################

import os
import sys
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from PyQt5.QtWidgets import (QApplication, QMainWindow, QWidget, QVBoxLayout, 
                            QHBoxLayout, QLabel, QLineEdit, QPushButton, 
                            QTextEdit, QFileDialog, QMessageBox, QProgressBar)
from PyQt5.QtCore import Qt, QThread, pyqtSignal, QMimeData  # 修正QMimeData的导入位置
from PyQt5.QtGui import QDragEnterEvent, QDropEvent  # 移除QMimeData的错误导入

class WorkerThread(QThread):
    """后台工作线程，避免UI卡顿"""
    update_signal = pyqtSignal(str)
    progress_signal = pyqtSignal(int)
    finish_signal = pyqtSignal(str)

    def __init__(self, project_dir, output_file):
        super().__init__()
        self.project_dir = project_dir
        self.output_file = output_file
        self.exclude_dirs = {'.git', '__pycache__', 'venv', 'env', 'node_modules', '.idea', '.vscode'}
        self.code_extensions = {
            '.py', '.java', '.cpp', '.c', '.h', '.hpp', '.js', '.ts', '.html', 
            '.css', '.php', '.rb', '.go', '.rs', '.json', '.jsonl', 
            '.xml', '.yaml', '.yml', '.sh', '.bash', '.sql', '.md', 
            '.txt', '.ini', '.conf'
        }

    def is_code_file(self, file_path):
        return Path(file_path).suffix.lower() in self.code_extensions

    def get_directory_structure(self, root_dir):
        structure = []
        root_dir = Path(root_dir).resolve()
        root_name = root_dir.name

        def add_directory(path, prefix=''):
            if path.name in self.exclude_dirs:
                return
                
            if path != root_dir:
                structure.append(f"{prefix}├── {path.name}/")
                new_prefix = prefix + "│   "
            else:
                structure.append(f"{root_name}/")
                new_prefix = "    "
            
            try:
                items = sorted(path.iterdir(), key=lambda x: (not x.is_dir(), x.name))
            except PermissionError:
                structure.append(f"{prefix}├── [无权限访问]")
                return
            
            for i, item in enumerate(items):
                if item.is_dir():
                    if i == len(items) - 1:
                        add_directory(item, prefix + "    ")
                    else:
                        add_directory(item, new_prefix)
                else:
                    if self.is_code_file(item):
                        if i == len(items) - 1:
                            structure.append(f"{prefix}└── {item.name}")
                        else:
                            structure.append(f"{prefix}├── {item.name}")
        
        add_directory(root_dir)
        return '\n'.join(structure)

    def collect_code_files(self, root_dir):
        code_files = []
        root_dir = Path(root_dir).resolve()
        total_files = 0
        processed = 0

        # 先计算总文件数
        for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(root_dir):
            dirpath = Path(dirpath)
            if dirpath.name in self.exclude_dirs:
                continue
            for filename in filenames:
                if self.is_code_file(Path(filename)):
                    total_files += 1

        # 收集文件内容
        for dirpath, dirnames, filenames in os.walk(root_dir):
            dirnames[:] = [d for d in dirnames if d not in self.exclude_dirs]
            
            for filename in filenames:
                file_path = Path(dirpath) / filename
                if self.is_code_file(file_path):
                    try:
                        encodings = ['utf-8', 'latin-1', 'utf-16']
                        content = None
                        
                        for encoding in encodings:
                            try:
                                with open(file_path, 'r', encoding=encoding) as f:
                                    content = f.read()
                                break
                            except UnicodeDecodeError:
                                continue
                        
                        if content is None:
                            content = f"[无法读取文件: {file_path} (编码问题)]"
                        
                        relative_path = file_path.relative_to(root_dir)
                        code_files.append((relative_path, content))
                        
                    except Exception as e:
                        code_files.append((file_path.relative_to(root_dir), f"[读取文件错误: {str(e)}]"))
                    
                    processed += 1
                    self.progress_signal.emit(int(processed / total_files * 100) if total_files > 0 else 100)
                    self.update_signal.emit(f"已处理: {processed}/{total_files} 文件")

        return code_files

    def run(self):
        try:
            self.update_signal.emit("正在生成目录结构...")
            dir_structure = self.get_directory_structure(self.project_dir)
            
            self.update_signal.emit("正在收集代码文件内容...")
            code_files = self.collect_code_files(self.project_dir)
            
            self.update_signal.emit("正在生成合并文件...")
            with open(self.output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write("="*80 + "\n")
                f.write("项目目录结构\n")
                f.write("="*80 + "\n\n")
                f.write(dir_structure + "\n\n")
                
                f.write("="*80 + "\n")
                f.write("代码文件内容\n")
                f.write("="*80 + "\n\n")
                
                for i, (rel_path, content) in enumerate(code_files, 1):
                    f.write(f"#"*80 + "\n")
                    f.write(f"# 文件 {i}/{len(code_files)}: {rel_path}\n")
                    f.write(f"#"*80 + "\n\n")
                    f.write(content + "\n\n")
            
            self.finish_signal.emit(str(self.output_file))
        except Exception as e:
            self.update_signal.emit(f"错误: {str(e)}")
            self.finish_signal.emit("error")

class ProjectCombinerUI(QMainWindow):
    """主窗口界面"""
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.init_ui()

    def init_ui(self):
        self.setWindowTitle("项目文件合并工具")
        self.setGeometry(100, 100, 800, 600)
        self.setAcceptDrops(True)

        # 主布局
        central_widget = QWidget()
        self.setCentralWidget(central_widget)
        main_layout = QVBoxLayout(central_widget)
        main_layout.setContentsMargins(20, 20, 20, 20)
        main_layout.setSpacing(15)

        # 项目路径输入区
        path_layout = QVBoxLayout()
        
        # 项目文件夹
        project_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.project_label = QLabel("项目文件夹:")
        self.project_input = QLineEdit()
        self.project_btn = QPushButton("浏览...")
        self.project_btn.clicked.connect(self.select_project_dir)
        project_layout.addWidget(self.project_label)
        project_layout.addWidget(self.project_input)
        project_layout.addWidget(self.project_btn)
        
        # 输出文件
        output_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.output_label = QLabel("输出文件:")
        self.output_input = QLineEdit()
        self.output_btn = QPushButton("浏览...")
        self.output_btn.clicked.connect(self.select_output_file)
        output_layout.addWidget(self.output_label)
        output_layout.addWidget(self.output_input)
        output_layout.addWidget(self.output_btn)
        
        path_layout.addLayout(project_layout)
        path_layout.addLayout(output_layout)
        main_layout.addLayout(path_layout)

        # 进度条
        self.progress_bar = QProgressBar()
        self.progress_bar.setVisible(False)
        main_layout.addWidget(self.progress_bar)

        # 日志区域
        self.log_label = QLabel("处理日志:")
        self.log_text = QTextEdit()
        self.log_text.setReadOnly(True)
        main_layout.addWidget(self.log_label)
        main_layout.addWidget(self.log_text)

        # 按钮区域
        btn_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.start_btn = QPushButton("开始生成")
        self.start_btn.clicked.connect(self.start_processing)
        self.copy_btn = QPushButton("复制输出路径")
        self.copy_btn.clicked.connect(self.copy_output_path)
        self.copy_btn.setEnabled(False)
        self.open_btn = QPushButton("打开输出文件")
        self.open_btn.clicked.connect(self.open_output_file)
        self.open_btn.setEnabled(False)
        
        btn_layout.addWidget(self.start_btn)
        btn_layout.addWidget(self.copy_btn)
        btn_layout.addWidget(self.open_btn)
        main_layout.addLayout(btn_layout)

    def dragEnterEvent(self, event: QDragEnterEvent):
        """处理拖入事件"""
        mime_data = event.mimeData()  # 显式获取mimeData
        if mime_data and mime_data.hasUrls():  # 先判断mime_data不为None
            url = mime_data.urls()[0]
            if url.isLocalFile():
                path = url.toLocalFile()
                if os.path.isdir(path):
                    event.acceptProposedAction()

    def dropEvent(self, event: QDropEvent):
        """处理放下事件"""
        mime_data = event.mimeData()  # 显式获取mimeData
        if mime_data and mime_data.hasUrls():  # 先判断mime_data不为None
            url = mime_data.urls()[0]
            path = url.toLocalFile()
            self.project_input.setText(path)
            # 自动填充输出路径
            if not self.output_input.text():
                self.output_input.setText(os.path.join(path, "project_combined.txt"))

    def select_project_dir(self):
        """选择项目文件夹"""
        dir_path = QFileDialog.getExistingDirectory(self, "选择项目文件夹")
        if dir_path:
            self.project_input.setText(dir_path)
            if not self.output_input.text():
                self.output_input.setText(os.path.join(dir_path, "project_combined.txt"))

    def select_output_file(self):
        """选择输出文件"""
        if not self.project_input.text():
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "警告", "请先选择项目文件夹")
            return
            
        default_dir = os.path.dirname(self.project_input.text())
        default_filename = os.path.join(default_dir, "project_combined.txt")
        
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getSaveFileName(
            self, "保存输出文件", default_filename, "文本文件 (*.txt);;所有文件 (*)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.output_input.setText(file_path)

    def start_processing(self):
        """开始处理"""
        project_dir = self.project_input.text().strip()
        output_file = self.output_input.text().strip()

        # 验证输入
        if not project_dir:
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "警告", "请输入项目文件夹路径")
            return
        
        if not os.path.isdir(project_dir):
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "警告", f"项目文件夹不存在: {project_dir}")
            return
            
        if not output_file:
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "警告", "请输入输出文件路径")
            return

        # 检查输出目录是否存在
        output_dir = os.path.dirname(output_file)
        if not os.path.exists(output_dir):
            try:
                os.makedirs(output_dir)
            except Exception as e:
                QMessageBox.critical(self, "错误", f"无法创建输出目录: {str(e)}")
                return

        # 准备处理
        self.log_text.clear()
        self.start_btn.setEnabled(False)
        self.progress_bar.setVisible(True)
        self.progress_bar.setValue(0)

        # 启动后台线程
        self.worker = WorkerThread(project_dir, output_file)
        self.worker.update_signal.connect(self.update_log)
        self.worker.progress_signal.connect(self.update_progress)
        self.worker.finish_signal.connect(self.process_finished)
        self.worker.start()

    def update_log(self, message):
        """更新日志"""
        self.log_text.append(message)
        # 滚动到底部
        self.log_text.moveCursor(self.log_text.textCursor().End)

    def update_progress(self, value):
        """更新进度条"""
        self.progress_bar.setValue(value)

    def process_finished(self, result):
        """处理完成"""
        self.start_btn.setEnabled(True)
        if result == "error":
            QMessageBox.critical(self, "错误", "处理过程中发生错误，请查看日志")
        else:
            self.update_log(f"处理完成！输出文件: {result}")
            self.output_file_path = result
            self.copy_btn.setEnabled(True)
            self.open_btn.setEnabled(True)

    def copy_output_path(self):
        """复制输出路径到剪贴板"""
        if hasattr(self, 'output_file_path'):
            clipboard = QApplication.clipboard()
            if clipboard:  # 先判断剪贴板不为None
                clipboard.setText(self.output_file_path)
                QMessageBox.information(self, "成功", "输出文件路径已复制到剪贴板")

    def open_output_file(self):
        """打开输出文件"""
        if hasattr(self, 'output_file_path') and os.path.exists(self.output_file_path):
            os.startfile(self.output_file_path)  # Windows系统
        else:
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "警告", "输出文件不存在")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = QApplication(sys.argv)
    window = ProjectCombinerUI()
    window.show()
    sys.exit(app.exec_())
